# File: r_list.txt

# Purpose: A parsable list of the Angband monsters

# This file is read by Angband on startup to initialize r_list

# Note that the uniques are just another monster race.


# Clear monsters acquire their attr from the item/floor below
# them, and use "light grey" for the recall window

# Multi-hued monsters have a flickering attr, and use "violet"
# for the recall window.  (There are other violet monsters!)

# Mushrooms look just like food, and use the "," symbol for
# both the recall window and for normal display

# Creeping coins look just like coins, and use the "$" symbol
# for both the recall window and for normal display

# Trappers and Lurkers get their attr/char from the "floor",
# and use a symbol of "." for the "recall" window

# Hack -- Mimics pretend to be (white) potions/scrolls/rings,
# depending on its level, thus they use "!"/"?"/"=" for both
# the recall window and for normal display.  This is a hack.



# Version stamp

V:2.7.8


##### The empty monster #####

N:0:(nobody)
I: :d:0:0d0:0:0:0:0:0:0
